    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2618761137639271899">From the very beginning, it impressed me with the author’s writing style and creativity in Dueling Fates. Stephanie M Allen grabs the reader’s attention from the start as we see the land of Erimos slowly being destroyed by their own king. The king’s advisor, Lord Savant Blackwood, takes matters into his own hands and kidnaps the prince for his own safety. Meanwhile, in the land of Neilos, siblings; Prince Fidelis, Princess Alena, and Princess Isemay learn of their mysterious heritage and the dan</span>
  <span id="freeText2618761137639271899" style="display:none">From the very beginning, it impressed me with the author’s writing style and creativity in Dueling Fates. Stephanie M Allen grabs the reader’s attention from the start as we see the land of Erimos slowly being destroyed by their own king. The king’s advisor, Lord Savant Blackwood, takes matters into his own hands and kidnaps the prince for his own safety. Meanwhile, in the land of Neilos, siblings; Prince Fidelis, Princess Alena, and Princess Isemay learn of their mysterious heritage and the danger they will face.<br /><br /> <br /><br />Dueling Fates is the beginning of a mesmerizing trilogy by Stephanie M Allen. I loved how Allen takes you to a world of kingdoms, dragons, and mystical creatures. There is a haunting undercurrent throughout this novel as the danger increases and the malicious plans come to light. The characters have vivid personalities that bring each one to life. Overall, this well-written novel keeps the reader captivated by the enchanting anticipation as events unfold. I was only disappointed when I reached the end and realized the next novel is not out yet.</span>

          </span>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3443800408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer789619440904125121">I absolutely love this book! There are three kingdoms. In each kingdom we get the point of you of what goes on with each kingdom’s main characters. This story not only had action, but it also had a little bit of magic, as well as mystery, and romance. I’m so excited to read the next book!</span>

<div id="review_3570708138" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3570708138" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3570708138?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3570708138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4068181201723525316">‘To be sold into marriage for the good of the kingdom’<br/><br/>Wyoming author Stephanie M. Allen earned her degree in English from California Baptist University in Riverside, California and to date has published five books – her four part HARMONY series and now DUELING FATES. <br/><br/>Creating a fantasy that takes place in a strange world becomes an invitation in Stephanie’s hands as she provides a map of the world of Erez, complete with named villages and mountains, on the page prior to her opening lines of the </span>
  <span id="freeText4068181201723525316" style="display:none">‘To be sold into marriage for the good of the kingdom’<br /><br />Wyoming author Stephanie M. Allen earned her degree in English from California Baptist University in Riverside, California and to date has published five books – her four part HARMONY series and now DUELING FATES. <br /><br />Creating a fantasy that takes place in a strange world becomes an invitation in Stephanie’s hands as she provides a map of the world of Erez, complete with named villages and mountains, on the page prior to her opening lines of the story: ‘Savant Blackwood coughed as he inhaled a lungful of thick, black smoke. He could barely distinguish between the glow of the crackling flames and the fiery orange sunset that lit the entire horizon. He dug his heels into his mare, urging her to an even faster gallop. Surely, he wasn’t too late to save at least part of the village. Surely he would find some survivors…’ That degree of both scenery painting and character building spills onto every page of this fantasy novel that deals with the fates of twin sisters.<br /><br />Ably offering a condensation of the plot that provides a map of this special place and time, the author presents the following: ‘In the world of Erez, three kingdoms share a tentative peace. In the far west, Princess Isemay yearns for much more than frilly dresses and etiquette classes. While her twin sister, Alena, prepares for life as a monarch in a neighboring kingdom, Isemay roams the woods with her loyal cheetah, hunting dagger strapped to her belt. It’s only when two surprising visitors arrive at the castle that Isemay must come to terms with her royal future – and a secret magical heritage. Now engaged to the king of the east, Isemay prepares for a position she never wanted. After saying good-bye to all that she loves, Princess Alena travels north in trepidation – fully prepared to marry a spoiled prince she does not desire and usurp the throne from his insane father who does not deserve it. But when tragedy strikes at her wedding ceremony and she is wrongfully imprisoned, she can only hope that her hurried plea for help will reach her father in time. Frantic to save her sister – and against the wishes of her betrothed – Isemay joins the army sent to free Alena. A mysterious encounter with a dragon in disguise leaves her with a warning that her life is in danger – but can it save her from the battle to come?’<br /><br />Fantasy fans, and those who welcome an escape to a magical place, will find this new novel satisfying. The author clearly has her talent for this genre. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4068181201723525316" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3538724607" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3538724607" />
    <a title="Alexandra Mack" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32697846-alexandra-mack"><img alt="Alexandra Mack" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541633201p2/32697846.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3538724607?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexandra Mack" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexandra Mack" href="/user/show/32697846-alexandra-mack">Alexandra Mack</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3538724607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11387025285603504476">I’ve been looking for a new high fantasy series to draw my attention, and these books seem to bring me just the universe I needed. Close-knit family with secrets? Check. Sweet romance? Check. Magic/magical creatures? Check. Interconnected kingdoms with their own histories and issues? Check. I was totally hooked into this story by the time I reached the middle of the novel. <br/><br/>Alena and Isemay are twins, but they are very different. As the eldest twin, Alena has been raised the most to be queen. Ise</span>
  <span id="freeText11387025285603504476" style="display:none">I’ve been looking for a new high fantasy series to draw my attention, and these books seem to bring me just the universe I needed. Close-knit family with secrets? Check. Sweet romance? Check. Magic/magical creatures? Check. Interconnected kingdoms with their own histories and issues? Check. I was totally hooked into this story by the time I reached the middle of the novel. <br /><br />Alena and Isemay are twins, but they are very different. As the eldest twin, Alena has been raised the most to be queen. Isemay still had to behave royally, but she had more freedom on how to live her life. Now they are both 17 and both have marriage prospects coming their way, but they have their own minds and hearts. Alena struggles to connect with a spoiled prince who will probably force her into a life that she hates in his stuffy castle. Isemay is more free-spirited than her sister, and she worries that her husband will separate her from the things she loves to do. Specifically, force her to be a queen who never gets to enjoy the beauty of nature and being active. Soon, these are the least of the worries of these two princesses. <br /><br />Alena and Isemay were some of the more realistic princess characters I have read in a while. Both were princesses, but they were normal teenaged girls first. They had their own unique personalities but this did not drive them away from one another. Alena and Isemay had one of the closest sister relationships I have read in a while. Also, they completely acted their age. They did not act older or younger than 17, they felt really relatable. I could understand why they were worried about their marriages, but they didn’t act like spoiled brats or put their kingdoms in danger. Overall, I fell in love with these characters. <br /><br />Out of all the love interests in this novel, my favorite was Jordan. He didn’t put Isemay into any situation where she was forced to be uncomfortable, and he truly wanted the best for her. They were honestly the only couple I truly rooted for in this novel, even though they all had their own chemistry. I can’t wait to see which couples will form and/or flourish in the next books of this series.<br /><br /><br />The only complaint I have about this book was that the synopsis tells the majority of the story. I was expecting the synopsis to only reveal the beginning portion of the book, but instead I got almost a summary of the entire book. I feel like this disappointed me once I realized that I knew about the majority of the storyline from the start. My suggestion would be to try to just read this book without reading the synopsis. <br /><br />I would recommend this to anyone looking for a new YA fantasy novel to read. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11387025285603504476" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14945272578461374360" style="display:none">Dueling Fates Tour held by @shannon_rrbooktours<br />🦄🦄🦄<br />In the world of Erez, three kingdoms share a tentative peace. In the far west, Princess Isemay yearns for much more than frilly dresses and etiquette classes. While her twin sister, Alena, prepares for life as a monarch in a neighboring kingdom, Isemay roams the woods with her loyal cheetah, hunting dagger strapped to her belt. It’s only when two surprising visitors arrive at the castle that Isemay must come to terms with her royal future – and a secret magical heritage. Now engaged to the king of the east, Isemay prepares for a position she never wanted.<br />After saying good-bye to all that she loves, Princess Alena travels north in trepidation – fully prepared to marry a spoiled prince she does not desire and usurp the throne from his insane father who does not deserve it. But when tragedy strikes at her wedding ceremony and she is wrongfully imprisoned, she can only hope that her hurried plea for help will reach her father in time.<br />Frantic to save her sister – and against the wishes of her betrothed – Isemay joins the army sent to free Alena. A mysterious encounter with a dragon in disguise leaves her with a warning that her life is in danger – but can it save her from the battle to come?<br />🦄🦄🦄<br />Dueling Fates by is a fairytale/fantasy novel by Stephanie M. Allen.<br />Giving us an enchanted look into a world of magic, this book will take you on a journey unlike any other.<br />The main characters have a tremendous amount of depth to it, and in some ways reminds me of another magical princess duo (if you know, you know). AND THERE'S ALSO A DRAGON! I mean, it's such a classic thing, but the implication of the dragon in the story spans across not only what we see in the classics, but gives it a new look. (Is this a metaphor or a real dragon? Read to find out😉)<br />And the romance....my heart couldn't take it. It wasn't cheesy, just pure and "spine tingly".<br />This book had me gripped from the very beginning with its intense opening shrouded in mystery and confusion and I couldn't put if down.<br />I have an evergrowing love for fairytale based stories and this one did not disappoint.<br />🦄🦄🦄<br />Rated 9.5/10<br />Melina L.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14945272578461374360" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText2020436831658978069" style="display:none">Dueling Fates is a great start to the series! I found myself easily pulled into the world and the lives of the characters. I love that all the elements you look for in a fantasy can be found in these pages; magic, mystery, and romance. <br />The only critique I would have is about the blurb. I generally try not to read the blurb before reading the book, I am someone who will choose a book based solely on the cover and/or author. The blurb for this book shares too much of the story, I would recommend condensing it. Otherwise, I found the book to be well written, the plot feels thought out and intentional, and the characters are fleshed out with many relatable characteristics. <br />I recommend this book to fantasy lovers and those looking to try fantasy! </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jBmHrb8gAeeMl3ercvoyFr0JEMj6EquMybPfY8IDcee2P+5/BH7Ijyu8w8qFDzjJa1b3ADSfJeuSzZnSD0CDfQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ngw/9SoWV97USw8CBnphUE2fJ5BbwyvMJU9XCicyQeqkKlYnkUietnNgu2Pxj2uPm8DAWJVOpat+MRG76nGzcA==')})
  }
//]]>
